            Neutron Scattering on Elemental Chromium.             2241100100004 
COMMENT    .Elastic Scattering is not Included in Cross-Sections  2241100100005 
AUTHOR     (D.Schmidt,W.Mannhart)                                 2241100100006 
INSTITUTE  (2GERPTB) PTB Braunschweig, Germany.                   2241100100007 
REFERENCE  (C,97TRIEST,1,407,199705)  Proc. Int. Conf. NDST       2241100100008 
                        Trieste, Italy (1997), Vol.1, P. 407-409  2241100100009 
           (R,INDC(GER)-044,1998) Progress Report INDC(GER)-044   2241100100010 
                                  (NEA/NSC/DOC(98)7) (1998) 44    2241100100011 
EXP-YEAR   (1995) 199505 Data Measured. 199711 - Data Published   2241100100012 
FACILITY   (CYCLO,2GERPTB) Turnable CV-28 compact cyclotron (1 ns 2241100100013 
            pulse width) and multi-angle neutron Time-Of-Flight   2241100100014 
            spectrometer.                                         2241100100015 
DETECTOR   (SCIN)  Five NE213 neutron detectors located behind    2241100100016 
             a massive collimator shielding in a distance of 1200 2241100100017 
             cm from the sample. The angle separation between the 2241100100018 
             detectors is 12.5 deg.                               2241100100019 
            Diameter 10.16 cm (D1)/ 25.40 cm (D2-D5),             2241100100020 
            Length 2.54 cm (D1)/ 5.08 cm (D2-D5).                 2241100100021 
            The angle region covered is 12.5 to 160 deg.          2241100100022 
            An additional NE213 detector was used as relative     2241100100023 
            fluence monitor, diameter 3.81 cm, length 3.81 cm.    2241100100024 
            The movable monitor (in a fixed distance of 651 cm)   2241100100025 
            was always in a position of 58.9 deg relative         2241100100026 
            to the beam axis.                                     2241100100027 
METHOD     (TOF) Time-of-flight, 12 m flight path.                2241100100028 
           (PSD) n/gamma discrimination with pulse shape analysis.2241100100029 
MONITOR    (1-H-1(N,EL)1-H-1,,DA)  Polyethylene sample            2241100100030 
              (diameter 24.56 mm, height 49.74 mm, mass 22.46 g,  2241100100031 
               H content 14.30 %)                                 2241100100032 
INC-SOURCE (D-D) Deuterium gas target, 1.0 cm in diameter and     2241100100033 
            3.0 cm in length, gas pressure 1.9-2.0 Hpa.           2241100100034 
            Mean neutron energy is defined within +/- 20 keV.     2241100100035 
SAMPLE     . Elemental chromium, cylindrical sample, 99.5% purity,2241100100036 
             diameter 25.0 mm, height 53.0 mm, mass 175.27 g,     2241100100037 
             placed 17.5 cm from the gas target centre.           2241100100038 
CORRECTION .Monte Carlo simulated TOF spectra of the complete     2241100100039 
            angular distribution were iteratively adjusted to     2241100100040 
            the measured TOF spectra. The simulation comprised    2241100100041 
            the neutron production in the gas target and the      2241100100042 
            scattering geometry between target, sample and        2241100100043 
            detectors.                                            2241100100044 
           .Parasitic neutrons from the D(d,np) breakup reaction  2241100100045 
            were simulated and subtracted. The data for the       2241100100046 
            simulation were adjusted by additional measurements   2241100100047 
            of the neutron scattering with a 4He(d,np) neutron    2241100100048 
            source (only breakup neutrons).                       2241100100049 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) Total errors comprise counting statistics and  2241100100050 
                   systematic contributions of                    2241100100051 
           (ERR-1)  - Detector Efficiency Error (2%),             2241100100052 
           (ERR-2)  - Angle Uncertainty    (0.2 DEG),             2241100100053 
           (ERR-3)  - Multiple Scattering Correction (5%).        2241100100054 
           (MONIT-ERR) - N-P Scattering Error (1%),               2241100100055 
           (ERR-4)  - An Additional Uncertainty of 5% of the      2241100100056 
                      Ratio  N-Bu/N-In is Taken Into Account      2241100100057 
            (N-BU = Subtracted fraction of scattered breakup      2241100100058 
             neutrons, N-IN = fraction of inelastically scattered 2241100100059 
             neutrons after breakup subtraction).                 2241100100060 
ANALYSIS    The double-differential inelastic cross sections were 2241100100061 
            extracted As elemental cross sections.                2241100100062
